< Text>
My first phenomenal experience with a car problem happened here, at AAMCO. (A rare occurrence in this day in age). These guys are trustworthy, and gain their client base by being honest and hard working. For once, I had the technicians trying to save me money, instead of scheming up ways in which to put more money in their pockets. I was given a quote on my brakes and rotors, and the specialist laid out on the table, all of my options. They explained to me, in thorough detail, what I would be getting instead of pawning me off to selecting the option most profitable for them. They insisted that I go with the most economical model and followed up with me to see if this was indeed my final decision. Before they made any adjustments, they wanted to make sure their client was most aware of what they were EXACTLY getting. They even offered to do a full inspection on my vehicle (when i had only gone in for brakes) and found that my frame was bent. As much of a travesty this was, they went out of their way and offered to tune up, and tighten my bushings, in order to lessen the effect of the bent frame from deteriorating the other parts. They were blatantly truthful in the situation and had informed me it would be best to leave the vehicle as-is, and to refrain from dumping any more money into the car. If you want a trustworthy company for a vehicle repair, and not have to worry about being bent over backwards and taken advantage of, AAMCO is your solution. Detail oriented and absolutely reliable!! I will be coming here for ALL of my future vehicle maintenance, as well as refer all of my friends and family to this place (even if it means driving 45 minutes to get there)!!!!</Text>

My first impression was a bit iffy because the location and sign doesn't reflect a modern vibe but that quickly changed once I stepped foot inside. The atmosphere is really cleanly & neat with plants near the entrance and spacious seating.

< Text>
I don't know what it is about this place that even the water tastes great. I know, it is freshness. Since day one, I have admired their kitchen philosophy which is fresh is always best. I come here often and try a different dish every time and I have yet to be disappointed. A staple for my family is Tom Yum Koon (shrimp and lemon broth) another of my favorites is Tamarind Fish, the burst of flavors out of that dish really stands out. Recommended as well, Tiger Beef, I have never tasted anything like it. Kids favorites chicken Pad See Eew.
Hands down the best Thai in the Valley. 5 stars does not do it justice if you combine the amazing service from the owner, to the best waitress, Vee. Family owned and operated.< /Text>

<Review>Everything we had was tasty, 4.5/5; .5+ for being family-owned and great service. I came in for dinner on a Friday night with family and ordered the Beef Jerky, Garlic Green Beans with Beef, Chicken and Shrimp Tom Kha, Panang Curry, and Crab Fried Rice. Each dish was made with care and so flavorful, couldn't stop eating even as I got full!

Crab fried rice used actual crab and the crab was all over the rice. The beef was seasoned amazingly (not too salty, which can be an issue at places trying to appeal to American tastebuds). Their approximation of the spiciness level in their food was average/fair: medium for curry had just a tiny kick; medium for tom kha was mostly mild--so if you like tom kha spicier than that maybe get spicy. I also had to try the Thai Iced Tea, which was very rich.

The place is family-owned and so far the food does show that care and authenticity. I really hope they do well. The ambience isn't anything notable negatively or positively either way--the spotlight is on the food which is what matters anyway...

I am hoping to come back and try more dishes. I would recommend this place if you like classic Thai food, and Thai food that isn't just lathered with sweet sauce and doesn't skimp on the quality ingredients.<//Review>< pics>
None</pics>

< review>
Ives is a nice pool but local families have always been disappointed with their limited open swim hours for families and general use. Even during open swim they still keep half the pool roped off for laps and this isn‚Äôt a very large pool. The drinking fountain on site seems like it‚Äôs from the 70‚Äôs and barely works. They only just installed an outdoor shower after all these years. There is very little shade to speak of. There is only a couple tables to sit at for such things as parties yet they have a large vacant lawn area. The snack bar can barely be called one. Considering it is the only public pool in Sebastopol they should really try to cater more evenly to the general public who just want to have fun in the heat of summer at their neighborhood pool. There is not a very welcoming feeling there. You always feel like they are doing you a favor by opening for very limited hours and months during the year for open swim.  The summer open swim hours start way too late after the heat has begun. The pool rules are also excessive and strict. Our family as well as many others more and more have to drive to Santa Rosa for a truly Fun pool experience. A very sad state of affairs for all the families dying in the heat of summers in Sebastopol.</review>

0x54d2eb14b3c38cf1:0x98dfcd187963d49e</Gmap_id>
<Pics>None< /Pics>< text>
Oh. My. Lord.  This place is stellar.

The food is out of this world. We had samosa + chole, and it was made in a chaat style. The samosas were hot, crunchy on the outside, and the potato filling inside was richly flavored, and not overly spicy. The chole were good, but the chutneys were the real clincher. Absolutely divine.

We also had some naan and palak paneer. The saag paneer was made with sarson (mustard leaf) saag, a little light on paneer. The saag was divine, just flavored right, hot and aromatic. Since this is a food truck, the naan was closer to rotis, but still very flavorful. You could close your eyes and be transported to Punjab.

Not only was the food amazing, but the hospitality was generous. After the meal, I asked the owner, "How much should I pay you" (in Hindi), he replied back in Hindi, "Give me whatever you thought that was worth." I haven't had such a warm experience in some of the best restaurants, let alone in a humble food truck.

This place is a gem. If you find yourself on I-5 heading North or South: do yourself a favor and get their samosas. If you can, thank the man for his oasis of flavor in a world of franchise restaurants.

The exterior is basic, the seating is a single portable table and four rickety chairs. Yet, this is among the best Indian food I have eaten in all of California: and that includes all the popular North-Indian restaurants in the South Bay and Los Angeles.

This place is a revelation. You can't judge a book by looking at the cover.<//text>

<username>Jason Berry</username><date>1583517722257<//date><rate>5</rate>< review>
Quite large laser tag maze with lots of space to hide and snipe.  Even at 100% capacity, there is lots of room to move.  The sensor vests and guns are a bit on the heavy side, but my 7 year old had no problem going the full 15 minutes.  There are a few video games, foosball, and 2 air hockey tables.  So not much else to do in the facility , but right around it, there is a food court and a Yogurtland downstairs. This location is very clean and not too loud.<//review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< text>
This place has been here ever since I can remember! It has always been good it's always been a place that's packed bcuz they have good food from burgers to tacos to pork chop dinner plates. If your a Monrovia native more than likely your going to run into someone you know here. Its especially busy on fridays when the Monrovia street fair is going on. You see all age groups and families in there. It's a cash place but they also have an atm there on the inside. There's 2 entrances one on Myrtle ave and the other one is on Olive which is the back entrance.</text>
